/*
The CALCULATE command controls the aggregation of leaf cells in the cube.
If the CALCULATE command is deleted or modified, the data within the cube is affected.
You should edit this command only if you manually specify how the cube is aggregated.
*/
CALCULATE;        
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Monthly Turns ]
 AS case when [Measures].[Period Business Days]=0 or [Measures].[Normal+Excess ]=0  then  0 else  ([Measures].[Monthly COGS]*[Measures].[Last12 Period Business Days]/[Measures].[Period Business Days])/([Measures].[Normal+Excess ])/[Measures].[Period Num Count] end, 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0.00;-#,##0.00", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;     
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Monthly COGS ]
 AS [Measures].[Monthly COGS], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;     
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Slow Value ]
 AS [Measures].[Slow Value]/[Measures].[Period Num Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;     
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Normal Value ]
 AS [Measures].[Normal Value]/[Measures].[Period Num Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;     
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Excess Value ]
 AS [Measures].[Excess Value]/[Measures].[Period Num Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;     
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Dead Value ]
 AS [Measures].[Dead Value]/[Measures].[Period Num Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;        
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Annual Turns ]
 AS case when (([Measures].[Last Excess Value]+[Measures].[Last Normal Value])/12) = 0 then 0 else [Measures].[Last12 Monthly COGS]/(([Measures].[Last Excess Value]+[Measures].[Last Normal Value])/12) end, 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0.00;-#,##0.00", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;        
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Total Inventory Turns ]
 AS case when [Measures].[Total Value ]=0 then 0 else ([Measures].[Monthly COGS]*[Measures].[Last12 Period Business Days]/[Measures].[Period Business Days]/[Measures].[Total Value ])/[Measures].[Period Num Count] end, 
FORMAT_STRING = "#,##0.00;-#,##0.00", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;          
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Total Value ]
 AS ([Measures].[Dead Value]+[Measures].[Slow Value]+[Measures].[Excess Value]+[Measures].[Normal Value])/[Measures].[Period Num Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "$#,##0.00;($#,##0.00)", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ;          
CREATE MEMBER CURRENTCUBE.[Measures].[Normal+Excess ]
 AS ([Measures].[Normal Value]+[Measures].[Excess Value])/[Measures].[Period Num Count], 
FORMAT_STRING = "Currency", 
VISIBLE = 1 ,  ASSOCIATED_MEASURE_GROUP = 'Inv Stat by Whse'  ; </Text>
                  </Command>
